## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

If MCP search returns no results:

2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching

4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

## SharedInformer Factory — File Map

The entire implementation lives in the kubernetes/kubernetes staging directory at `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/` (the canonical source that gets published as `k8s.io/client-go`).

### Core infrastructure (`tools/cache/`)
| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `shared_informer.go` | `SharedInformer`/`SharedIndexInformer` interfaces, `WaitForCacheSync` |
| `controller.go` | `Controller` — drives the Reflector→DeltaFIFO→Store loop |
| `reflector.go` | `Reflector` — performs List+Watch against the API server |
| `listwatch.go` | `ListWatch` — the concrete REST-backed ListerWatcher |
| `store.go` | `Store`/`Indexer` interfaces — the local in-memory cache |
| `thread_safe_store.go` | `ThreadSafeStore` — concurrent backing map |
| `delta_fifo.go` | `DeltaFIFO` — event buffer between Reflector and store |
| `synctrack/synctrack.go` + `lazy.go` | Per-item sync tracking for `HasSynced` |

### Factory registration (`informers/`)
| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `informers/factory.go` | `SharedInformerFactory` — `NewSharedInformerFactory`, `InformerFor`, `Start`, `WaitForCacheSync` |
| `informers/generic.go` | `ForResource` dispatch by GVR |
| `informers/internalinterfaces/factory_interfaces.go` | Internal `SharedInformerFactory` mini-interface |
| `informers/{group}/{version}/*.go` | Per-resource informer registrations (all API groups) |

### Variant factories
- `dynamic/dynamicinformer/` — `DynamicSharedInformerFactory` for unstructured resources
- `metadata/metadatainformer/` — `metadataSharedInformerFactory` for partial-metadata informers

lives entirely under the staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/ directory, which is the canonical source for the published k8s.io/client-go module.\\n\\n## Core cache and sync infrastructure (tools/cache)\\n\\n- **shared_informer.go**: Defines SharedInformer and SharedIndexInformer interfaces, the sharedIndexInformer struct that wires together the Controller+DeltaFIFO+store pipeline, WaitForCacheSync/WaitForNamedCacheSync for blocking until the local cache is in sync with the API server.\\n- **controller.go**: The Controller type that drives a Reflector->DeltaFIFO->store loop. NewInformer and NewIndexerInformer are the lower-level constructors.\\n- **reflector.go**: Reflector implements the list-watch loop: calls ListWatch.List to do an initial bulk load, then ListWatch.Watch to stream delta events, populating the DeltaFIFO queue.\\n- **listwatch.go**: ListWatch struct and NewListWatchFromClient -- the concrete ListerWatcher backed by a REST client that issues List and Watch API calls to the Kubernetes API server.\\n- **store.go**: Store and Indexer interfaces; cache struct (thread-safe store backed by threadSafeMap) is the local in-memory cache.\\n- **thread_safe_store.go**: ThreadSafeStore -- the low-level concurrent map used by the cache store.\\n- **delta_fifo.go**: DeltaFIFO -- the FIFO queue that buffers Add/Update/Delete/Sync/Replace events from the Reflector before they are processed into the store.\\n- **index.go**: Indexer interface and MetaNamespaceIndexFunc helper.\\n- **listers.go**: GenericLister/GenericNamespaceLister helpers used by typed listers.\\n- **fifo.go**: Classic FIFO queue.\\n- **heap.go**: Heap-based priority queue.\\n- **object-names.go**: Helpers for extracting object keys.\\n- **mutation_cache.go / mutation_detector.go**: Optional overlay cache for optimistic mutation tracking.\\n- **undelta_store.go**: UndeltaStore wraps a store to re-list objects on each event.\\n- **expiration_cache.go / expiration_cache_fakes.go / fake_custom_store.go**: Expiration-aware cache implementations.\\n- **reflector_metrics.go / reflector_data_consistency_detector.go**: Metrics and data-consistency helpers for the Reflector.\\n- **retry_with_deadline.go**: Utility for retrying with a deadline used by the Reflector.\\n- **synctrack/synctrack.go / synctrack/lazy.go**: AsyncTracker and Lazy -- fine-grained per-item sync-state tracking used by sharedIndexInformer to implement HasSynced.\\n\\n## SharedInformerFactory (informers/)\\n\\n- **informers/factory.go**: Main SharedInformerFactory interface + sharedInformerFactory struct. Provides NewSharedInformerFactory, NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions, InformerFor (registers and caches informers by type), Start (launches goroutines), and WaitForCacheSync.\\n- **informers/generic.go**: ForResource method -- dispatches to the correct typed informer by GVR.\\n- **informers/internalinterfaces/factory_interfaces.go**: SharedInformerFactory mini-interface (just Start + InformerFor) used internally to avoid import cycles; NewInformerFunc type alias.\\n- **informers/doc.go**: Package documentation.\\n\\n## Dynamic and Metadata informers\\n\\n- **dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go + interface.go**: DynamicSharedInformerFactory for unstructured dynamic resources.\\n- **metadata/metadatainformer/informer.go + interface.go**: metadataSharedInformerFactory for partial-metadata-only informers.\\n\\n## Per-resource informer registrations (informers/{group}/{version}/{resource}.go)\\n\\nEach file under informers/admissionregistration/, informers/apps/, informers/autoscaling/, informers/batch/, informers/certificates/, informers/coordination/, informers/core/, informers/discovery/, informers/events/, informers/extensions/, informers/flowcontrol/, informers/networking/, informers/node/, informers/policy/, informers/rbac/, informers/resource/, informers/scheduling/, informers/storage/, and informers/storagemigration/ registers one Kubernetes resource type with the factory via factory.InformerFor(obj, newFunc), where newFunc calls NewFilteredXxxInformer which builds a ListWatch from the typed client and constructs a NewSharedIndexInformer.\"\n}\n",

lives entirely under the staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/ directory, which is the canonical source for the published k8s.io/client-go module.\\n\\n## Core cache and sync infrastructure (tools/cache)\\n\\n- **shared_informer.go**: Defines SharedInformer and SharedIndexInformer interfaces, the sharedIndexInformer struct that wires together the Controller+DeltaFIFO+store pipeline, WaitForCacheSync/WaitForNamedCacheSync for blocking until the local cache is in sync with the API server.\\n- **controller.go**: The Controller type that drives a Reflector->DeltaFIFO->store loop. NewInformer and NewIndexerInformer are the lower-level constructors.\\n- **reflector.go**: Reflector implements the list-watch loop: calls ListWatch.List to do an initial bulk load, then ListWatch.Watch to stream delta events, populating the DeltaFIFO queue.\\n- **listwatch.go**: ListWatch struct and NewListWatchFromClient -- the concrete ListerWatcher backed by a REST client that issues List and Watch API calls to the Kubernetes API server.\\n- **store.go**: Store and Indexer interfaces; cache struct (thread-safe store backed by threadSafeMap) is the local in-memory cache.\\n- **thread_safe_store.go**: ThreadSafeStore -- the low-level concurrent map used by the cache store.\\n- **delta_fifo.go**: DeltaFIFO -- the FIFO queue that buffers Add/Update/Delete/Sync/Replace events from the Reflector before they are processed into the store.\\n- **index.go**: Indexer interface and MetaNamespaceIndexFunc helper.\\n- **listers.go**: GenericLister/GenericNamespaceLister helpers used by typed listers.\\n- **fifo.go**: Classic FIFO queue.\\n- **heap.go**: Heap-based priority queue.\\n- **object-names.go**: Helpers for extracting object keys.\\n- **mutation_cache.go / mutation_detector.go**: Optional overlay cache for optimistic mutation tracking.\\n- **undelta_store.go**: UndeltaStore wraps a store to re-list objects on each event.\\n- **expiration_cache.go / expiration_cache_fakes.go / fake_custom_store.go**: Expiration-aware cache implementations.\\n- **reflector_metrics.go / reflector_data_consistency_detector.go**: Metrics and data-consistency helpers for the Reflector.\\n- **retry_with_deadline.go**: Utility for retrying with a deadline used by the Reflector.\\n- **synctrack/synctrack.go / synctrack/lazy.go**: AsyncTracker and Lazy -- fine-grained per-item sync-state tracking used by sharedIndexInformer to implement HasSynced.\\n\\n## SharedInformerFactory (informers/)\\n\\n- **informers/factory.go**: Main SharedInformerFactory interface + sharedInformerFactory struct. Provides NewSharedInformerFactory, NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions, InformerFor (registers and caches informers by type), Start (launches goroutines), and WaitForCacheSync.\\n- **informers/generic.go**: ForResource method -- dispatches to the correct typed informer by GVR.\\n- **informers/internalinterfaces/factory_interfaces.go**: SharedInformerFactory mini-interface (just Start + InformerFor) used internally to avoid import cycles; NewInformerFunc type alias.\\n- **informers/doc.go**: Package documentation.\\n\\n## Dynamic and Metadata informers\\n\\n- **dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go + interface.go**: DynamicSharedInformerFactory for unstructured dynamic resources.\\n- **metadata/metadatainformer/informer.go + interface.go**: metadataSharedInformerFactory for partial-metadata-only informers.\\n\\n## Per-resource informer registrations (informers/{group}/{version}/{resource}.go)\\n\\nEach file under informers/admissionregistration/, informers/apps/, informers/autoscaling/, informers/batch/, informers/certificates/, informers/coordination/, informers/core/, informers/discovery/, informers/events/, informers/extensions/, informers/flowcontrol/, informers/networking/, informers/node/, informers/policy/, informers/rbac/, informers/resource/, informers/scheduling/, informers/storage/, and informers/storagemigration/ registers one Kubernetes resource type with the factory via factory.InformerFor(obj, newFunc), where newFunc calls NewFilteredXxxInformer which builds a ListWatch from the typed client and constructs a NewSharedIndexInformer.\"\n}\n",
